INDUSTRIES DEPARTMENT
ACQUISITION OF LANDS.
FORM VI
DECLARATION
UNIT - I, BLOCK 1 - II
[G.O.Ms. No. 70, Industries (GIM) Dept, 10th February 2021, ij 28, rh®tç, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052]
No. II(2)/IND/94(b-1)/2021.
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of 677.30.55 hectares of land is required in the 
Madavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi District for a public purpose, namely, establishing 
a new launch station for SSLV in favour of ISRO and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR.
Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 109.88.50 hectares 
in Block 1 to 11, Unit-I is under acquisition for the above said project in the Madavankurichi Village in 
Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi District whose detailed description is as follows:
TAMIL  NADU
GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

This declaration is made under Section 19 (1) read with sub-section (4) of Section 40 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land 
Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). There is no project aﬀ ected family in Block No.1 to 11 of Unit-I and hence the 
Elements of rehabilitation and resettlement entitlements under Second Schedule and provision of infrastructural amenities under Third Schedule of Right to Fair 
Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) shall not apply. 
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed. 
         
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition oﬃ  cer / District Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer 
(L.A), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur on any working day.
N. MURUGANANDAM,
Principal Secretary to Government.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
INDUSTRIES DEPARTMENT
FORM VI
DECLARATION
UNIT-II, Block 1-13
[G.O.Ms. No. 71, Industries (GIM) Dept, 10th February 2021, ij 28, rh®tç, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052]
No. II(2)/IND/92(b-2)/2021.
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of 677.30.55 hectares of land is required in the Madavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi 
District for a public purpose, namely, establishing a new launch station for SSLV infavour of ISRO and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR.
Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 113.99.77 hectares in Block 1 to 13, Unit-II is under acquisition for the above 
said project in the Madavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made under Section 19 (1) read with sub-section (4) of Section 40 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land 
Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). There is no project aﬀ ected family in Block No.1 to 13 of Unit-II and hence 
the Elements of rehabilitation and resettlement entitlements under Second Schedule and provision of infrastructural amenities under Third Schedule of Right to 
Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) shall not apply. 
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition oﬃ  cer / District Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer 
(L.A), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur on any working day.
 N.MURUGANANDAM,
Principal Secretary to Government.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY 
211
INDUSTRIES DEPARTMENT
FORM VI
DECLARATION
UNIT-VII, Block 1-11
[G.O.Ms. No. 72, Industries (GIM) Dept, 10th February 2021, ij 28, rh®tç, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No. II(2)/IND/94(b-3)/2021.
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of 677.30.55 hectares of land is required in the Madavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi 
District for a public purpose, namely, establishing a new launch station for SSLV in favour of ISRO and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR.
Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 120.63.50 hectares in Block 1 to 11, Unit-VII is under acquisition for the 
above said project in the Madavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made under Section 19 (1) read with sub-section (4) of Section 40 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land 
Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). There is no project aﬀ ected family in Block No.1 to 11 of Unit-VII and hence 
the Elements of rehabilitation and resettlement entitlements under Second Schedule and provision of infrastructural amenities under Third Schedule of Right to 
Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) shall not apply. 
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.  
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition oﬃ  cer / District Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer 
(L.A), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur on any working day.
 N. MURUGANANDAM,
Principal Secretary to Government.
